https://github.com/juvenn/juvenn.github.io/blob/bc45aa1519558231d352b845e2301b5ba13e5cf7/src/routes/sitemap.xml/%2Bserver.js

```
# Comprehensive Design & Technical SEO Blueprint for Women's Wellness Website

---

## SECTION 1: Professional Female-Centric UI/UX Design & Branding

### 1.1 Visual Palette & Typography

**Color Palette (Modern, Premium, Wellness-Focused):**

| Color Role | Hex Code | RGB | Usage | Psychology |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Primary Brand** | `#8BA888` | (139, 168, 136) | Buttons, CTA, accents | Calming, natural, growth |
| **Secondary Accent** | `#B99B6B` | (185, 155, 107) | Highlights, badges, warmth | Luxury, grounding, trust |
| **Rose Accent** | `#D9876D` | (217, 135, 109) | Energy, urgency, passion | Movement, vitality, femininity |
| **Soft Lavender** | `#E8D9F0` | (232, 217, 240) | Subtle backgrounds, hover | Peace, rest, premium feel |
| **Warm Neutral (Bone)** | `#F5F1ED` | (245, 241, 237) | Page backgrounds, clean space | Modern, minimal, sophisticated |
| **Text (Ink)** | `#3D443D` | (61, 68, 61) | Body text, readability | Professional, grounded |
| **Muted Gray** | `#9A8E7E` | (154, 142, 126) | Secondary text, captions | Approachable, softer |

**Typography (Google Fonts Integration):**

```html
<!-- Add to <head> -->
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600;700&family=Playfair+Display:wght@600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
```

| Font | Role | Weight | Usage |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Playfair Display** | Serif Headline | 600–700 | Main headlines, hero section, premium feel |
| **Inter** | Sans-serif Body | 400–700 | Body text, CTAs, UI elements, readable at any size |

**Font Sizing Scale (Responsive):**
- **H1 (Hero):** 48px (mobile) → 64px (desktop)
- **H2 (Section):** 28px (mobile) → 42px (desktop)
- **H3 (Card Title):** 20px (mobile) → 24px (desktop)
- **Body:** 16px (mobile) → 18px (desktop)
- **Small Text:** 14px (mobile) → 16px (desktop)

---

### 1.2 Layout & Elements

**Landing Page Structure (High-Trust, Conversion-Optimized):**

```
1. HERO SECTION (Above the fold)
   ├─ Headline (Playfair Display, 64px, left-aligned)
   ├─ Subheading (Emotional, empathetic hook)
   ├─ Primary CTA Button (Sage green, 16px, rounded-full)
   ├─ Social Proof (Avatar stack + "50,000+ women reclaimed energy")
   └─ Hero Image (Right side, authentic woman, natural lighting, peaceful expression)

2. TRUST BADGES SECTION
   ├─ 5-star rating + review count (3,842 reviews)
   ├─ Verified checkmarks
   ├─ 30-day money-back guarantee badge
   └─ SSL/Security badge

3. PROBLEM-AGITATION SECTION
   ├─ "The Struggles Are Real" (H2)
   ├─ 3 pain-point cards with icons (Energy, Sleep, Confidence)
   └─ Emotional copy validating her struggles

4. SOLUTION-BENEFITS SECTION
   ├─ "Your Personalized Blueprint" (H2)
   ├─ 4 benefit cards (Energy, Sleep, Confidence, Body)
   └─ Light background color (Lavender or Bone)

5. HOW IT WORKS
   ├─ 3-step timeline (Quiz → Analysis → Personalized Plan)
   └─ Simple, clean icons + minimal copy

6. TESTIMONIALS / SOCIAL PROOF
   ├─ Before/After Slider (drag-to-compare)
   ├─ 3–6 testimonial cards (avatar, name, location, result, 5-star rating)
   └─ Video testimonial embed (optional, high-impact)

7. FAQ SECTION
   ├─ 5–7 collapsible accordion items
   └─ Common objection handlers (No diet, not restrictive, etc.)

8. FINAL CTA
   ├─ Bold headline ("Ready to Feel Like Yourself Again?")
   ├─ Primary button (Sage green, large, high contrast)
   └─ Guarantee statement (30-day money-back, no questions)
```

**Quiz Page Layout (Engagement-First):**

```
1. PROGRESS BAR
   ├─ Visual indicator (current question / total 13)
   └─ Percentage filled (0%–100%)

2. QUESTION CARD
   ├─ Large, readable question (20px–24px, Playfair or Inter)
   ├─ Supportive subtext (optional, smaller font)
   └─ Answer options (buttons, radio, slider—contextual)

3. ANSWER BUTTONS
   ├─ Light gray background (hover: sage green)
   ├─ Rounded corners (12px–16px border radius)
   ├─ Smooth transitions (250ms)
   └─ Mobile: full-width, stacked vertically

4. NAVIGATION
   ├─ "Back" button (quiet gray, left-aligned)
   ├─ "Next" / "Continue" button (sage green, prominent, right-aligned)
   └─ Mobile: bottom sticky bar with both buttons

5. EMOTIONAL PROGRESS
   ├─ Supportive microcopy ("You're doing great!")
   ├─ Progress celebrations (phases completed)
   └─ Optional progress emojis (✓, 🌱, 💪)
```

**Product / Service Cards (High-Converting):**

```
CARD STRUCTURE
├─ Image or icon (aspect ratio 3:2 or 16:9)
├─ Category badge (soft green background, small text)
├─ Title (H3, Playfair Display)
├─ Description (2–3 lines, 16px Inter)
├─ Primary benefit (italic, 14px, sage green text)
├─ Key features (3–5 bullet points, checkmark icons)
├─ Price section
│  ├─ Current price (large, bold, sage green)
│  ├─ Strikethrough old price (muted gray)
│  └─ Savings callout (rose red background)
├─ Trust badges (30-day guarantee, instant access, SSL)
└─ CTA button (Sage green, full-width on mobile)
```

---

**Photography & Imagery:**

| Category | Style | Tone | Examples |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Hero Images** | Authentic, natural lighting, minimalist background | Peaceful, confident, real | Woman in yoga pose, sunrise in home, candid smile |
| **Testimonial Avatars** | Diverse body types, ages 25–55, genuine expressions | Relatable, warm, trustworthy | Real photos, no excessive filtering |

| **Video Content** | 15–60 seconds, testimonials & quick demos | Authentic, fast-paced, captions included | Woman doing yoga, short results montage, testimonial |

**Image Optimization:**
- Format: WebP (primary), JPEG fallback
- Sizes: Serve responsive images (480px, 768px, 1200px, 1920px)
- Alt text: Descriptive, keyword-rich, actionable
- Lazy loading: Enable for below-fold images

**Typography in Images:**
- Overlay text: Use Playfair Display in white or sage green
- Contrast ratio: Minimum 4.5:1 for accessibility

# Comprehensive Design & Technical SEO Blueprint for Women's Wellness Website

---

## SECTION 1: Professional Female-Centric UI/UX Design & Branding

### 1.1 Visual Palette & Typography

**Color Palette (Modern, Premium, Wellness-Focused):**

| Color Role | Hex Code | RGB | Usage | Psychology |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Primary Brand** | `#8BA888` | (139, 168, 136) | Buttons, CTA, accents | Calming, natural, growth |
| **Secondary Accent** | `#B99B6B` | (185, 155, 107) | Highlights, badges, warmth | Luxury, grounding, trust |
| **Rose Accent** | `#D9876D` | (217, 135, 109) | Energy, urgency, passion | Movement, vitality, femininity |
| **Soft Lavender** | `#E8D9F0` | (232, 217, 240) | Subtle backgrounds, hover | Peace, rest, premium feel |
| **Warm Neutral (Bone)** | `#F5F1ED` | (245, 241, 237) | Page backgrounds, clean space | Modern, minimal, sophisticated |
| **Text (Ink)** | `#3D443D` | (61, 68, 61) | Body text, readability | Professional, grounded |
| **Muted Gray** | `#9A8E7E` | (154, 142, 126) | Secondary text, captions | Approachable, softer |

**Typography (Google Fonts Integration):**

```html
<!-- Add to <head> -->
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600;700&family=Playfair+Display:wght@600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
```

| Font | Role | Weight | Usage |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Playfair Display** | Serif Headline | 600–700 | Main headlines, hero section, premium feel |
| **Inter** | Sans-serif Body | 400–700 | Body text, CTAs, UI elements, readable at any size |

**Font Sizing Scale (Responsive):**
- **H1 (Hero):** 48px (mobile) → 64px (desktop)
- **H2 (Section):** 28px (mobile) → 42px (desktop)
- **H3 (Card Title):** 20px (mobile) → 24px (desktop)
- **Body:** 16px (mobile) → 18px (desktop)
- **Small Text:** 14px (mobile) → 16px (desktop)

---

### 1.2 Layout & Elements

**Landing Page Structure (High-Trust, Conversion-Optimized):**

```
1. HERO SECTION (Above the fold)
   ├─ Headline (Playfair Display, 64px, left-aligned)
   ├─ Subheading (Emotional, empathetic hook)
   ├─ Primary CTA Button (Sage green, 16px, rounded-full)
   ├─ Social Proof (Avatar stack + "50,000+ women reclaimed energy")
   └─ Hero Image (Right side, authentic woman, natural lighting, peaceful expression)

2. TRUST BADGES SECTION
   ├─ 5-star rating + review count (3,842 reviews)
   ├─ Verified checkmarks
   ├─ 30-day money-back guarantee badge
   └─ SSL/Security badge

3. PROBLEM-AGITATION SECTION
   ├─ "The Struggles Are Real" (H2)
   ├─ 3 pain-point cards with icons (Energy, Sleep, Confidence)
   └─ Emotional copy validating her struggles

4. SOLUTION-BENEFITS SECTION
   ├─ "Your Personalized Blueprint" (H2)
   ├─ 4 benefit cards (Energy, Sleep, Confidence, Body)
   └─ Light background color (Lavender or Bone)

5. HOW IT WORKS
   ├─ 3-step timeline (Quiz → Analysis → Personalized Plan)
   └─ Simple, clean icons + minimal copy

6. TESTIMONIALS / SOCIAL PROOF
   ├─ Before/After Slider (drag-to-compare)
   ├─ 3–6 testimonial cards (avatar, name, location, result, 5-star rating)
   └─ Video testimonial embed (optional, high-impact)

7. FAQ SECTION
   ├─ 5–7 collapsible accordion items
   └─ Common objection handlers (No diet, not restrictive, etc.)

8. FINAL CTA
   ├─ Bold headline ("Ready to Feel Like Yourself Again?")
   ├─ Primary button (Sage green, large, high contrast)
   └─ Guarantee statement (30-day money-back, no questions)
```

**Quiz Page Layout (Engagement-First):**

```
1. PROGRESS BAR
   ├─ Visual indicator (current question / total 13)
   └─ Percentage filled (0%–100%)

2. QUESTION CARD
   ├─ Large, readable question (20px–24px, Playfair or Inter)
   ├─ Supportive subtext (optional, smaller font)
   └─ Answer options (buttons, radio, slider—contextual)

3. ANSWER BUTTONS
   ├─ Light gray background (hover: sage green)
   ├─ Rounded corners (12px–16px border radius)
   ├─ Smooth transitions (250ms)
   └─ Mobile: full-width, stacked vertically

4. NAVIGATION
   ├─ "Back" button (quiet gray, left-aligned)
   ├─ "Next" / "Continue" button (sage green, prominent, right-aligned)
   └─ Mobile: bottom sticky bar with both buttons

5. EMOTIONAL PROGRESS
   ├─ Supportive microcopy ("You're doing great!")
   ├─ Progress celebrations (phases completed)
   └─ Optional progress emojis (✓, 🌱, 💪)
```

**Product / Service Cards (High-Converting):**

```
CARD STRUCTURE
├─ Image or icon (aspect ratio 3:2 or 16:9)
├─ Category badge (soft green background, small text)
├─ Title (H3, Playfair Display)
├─ Description (2–3 lines, 16px Inter)
├─ Primary benefit (italic, 14px, sage green text)
├─ Key features (3–5 bullet points, checkmark icons)
├─ Price section
│  ├─ Current price (large, bold, sage green)
│  ├─ Strikethrough old price (muted gray)
│  └─ Savings callout (rose red background)
├─ Trust badges (30-day guarantee, instant access, SSL)
└─ CTA button (Sage green, full-width on mobile)
```

---

### 1.3 Media Guidelines

**Photography & Imagery:**

| Category | Style | Tone | Examples |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Hero Images** | Authentic, natural lighting, minimalist background | Peaceful, confident, real | Woman in yoga pose, sunrise in home, candid smile |
| **Testimonial Avatars** | Diverse body types, ages 25–55, genuine expressions | Relatable, warm, trustworthy | Real photos, no excessive filtering |
| **Before/After** | Dignified, empowering (not shocking), same clothing/angle | Transformation, progress, hope | Posture improvement, visible confidence, not just weight |
| **Icon Usage** | Minimalist line-drawn icons, sage green or rose | Friendly, modern, non-clinical | Energy (lightning bolt), sleep (moon), confidence (heart) |
| **Video Content** | 15–60 seconds, testimonials & quick demos | Authentic, fast-paced, captions included | Woman doing yoga, short results montage, testimonial |

**Image Optimization:**
- Format: WebP (primary), JPEG fallback
- Sizes: Serve responsive images (480px, 768px, 1200px, 1920px)
- Alt text: Descriptive, keyword-rich, actionable
- Lazy loading: Enable for below-fold images

**Typography in Images:**
- Overlay text: Use Playfair Display in white or sage green
- Contrast ratio: Minimum 4.5:1 for accessibility

---

## SECTION 2: Technical SEO, Indexing & Crawling Files

### 2.1 robots.txt File

**Purpose:** Allow search engines to crawl public pages while protecting sensitive areas.

**File Location:** `robots.txt` in the root directory (e.g., `https://yoursite.com/robots.txt`)

```plaintext
# FitFeky Robots File
# Last Updated: May 2026
# Purpose: Allow search engines to crawl public pages; protect admin and checkout areas

User-agent: *
Allow: /
Allow: /blog/
Allow: /quiz/
Allow: /shop/
Allow: /pages/
Allow: /products/
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Disallow sensitive pages and directories
Disallow: /admin/
Disallow: /dashboard/
Disallow: /checkout/
Disallow: /cart/
Disallow: /account/
Disallow: /private/
Disallow: /api/
Disallow: /internal/
Disallow: /*.json$
Disallow: /*.pdf$
Disallow: /search?
Disallow: /*?*sort=
Disallow: /*?*filter=
Disallow: /temp/
Disallow: /backup/
Disallow: /cache/

# Allow specific bot behaviors
Allow: /robots.txt
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Crawl-Delay & Rate Limiting
Crawl-delay: 1
Request-rate: 10/1s

# Google-specific directives
User-agent: Googlebot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 0.5

# Bing-specific directives
User-agent: Bingbot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 1

# Disallow other bots (optional, strict mode)
User-agent: MJ12bot
User-agent: AhrefsBot
User-agent: SemrushBot
Disallow: /

# Sitemap location (critical for indexing)
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml
```

---

### 2.2 XML Sitemap Architecture

**Primary Sitemap (Main Index):**

**File:** `sitemap.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<sitemapindex xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">
  <!-- Main pages sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-main.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Blog/content sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Products/services sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Quiz landing pages sitemap (if quiz results create unique pages) -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-quiz.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
</sitemapindex>
```

**Main Pages Sitemap:**

**File:** `sitemap-main.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9"
        xmlns:image="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-image/1.1"
        xmlns:video="http://
```

4. NAVIGATION
   ├─ "Back" button (quiet gray, left-aligned)
   ├─ "Next" / "Continue" button (sage green, prominent, right-aligned)
   └─ Mobile: bottom sticky bar with both buttons

5. EMOTIONAL PROGRESS
   ├─ Supportive microcopy ("You're doing great!")
   ├─ Progress celebrations (phases completed)
   └─ Optional progress emojis (✓, 🌱, 💪)
```

**Product / Service Cards (High-Converting):**

```
CARD STRUCTURE
├─ Image or icon (aspect ratio 3:2 or 16:9)
├─ Category badge (soft green background, small text)
├─ Title (H3, Playfair Display)
├─ Description (2–3 lines, 16px Inter)
├─ Primary benefit (italic, 14px, sage green text)
├─ Key features (3–5 bullet points, checkmark icons)
├─ Price section
│  ├─ Current price (large, bold, sage green)
│  ├─ Strikethrough old price (muted gray)
│  └─ Savings callout (rose red background)
├─ Trust badges (30-day guarantee, instant access, SSL)
└─ CTA button (Sage green, full-width on mobile)
```

---

### 1.3 Media Guidelines

**Photography & Imagery:**

| Category | Style | Tone | Examples |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Hero Images** | Authentic, natural lighting, minimalist background | Peaceful, confident, real | Woman in yoga pose, sunrise in home, candid smile |
| **Testimonial Avatars** | Diverse body types, ages 25–55, genuine expressions | Relatable, warm, trustworthy | Real photos, no excessive filtering |
| **Before/After** | Dignified, empowering (not shocking), same clothing/angle | Transformation, progress, hope | Posture improvement, visible confidence, not just weight |
| **Icon Usage** | Minimalist line-drawn icons, sage green or rose | Friendly, modern, non-clinical | Energy (lightning bolt), sleep (moon), confidence (heart) |
| **Video Content** | 15–60 seconds, testimonials & quick demos | Authentic, fast-paced, captions included | Woman doing yoga, short results montage, testimonial |

**Image Optimization:**
- Format: WebP (primary), JPEG fallback
- Sizes: Serve responsive images (480px, 768px, 1200px, 1920px)
- Alt text: Descriptive, keyword-rich, actionable
- Lazy loading: Enable for below-fold images

**Typography in Images:**
- Overlay text: Use Playfair Display in white or sage green
- Contrast ratio: Minimum 4.5:1 for accessibility

---

## SECTION 2: Technical SEO, Indexing & Crawling Files

### 2.1 robots.txt File

**Purpose:** Allow search engines to crawl public pages while protecting sensitive areas.

**File Location:** `robots.txt` in the root directory (e.g., `https://yoursite.com/robots.txt`)

```plaintext
# FitFeky Robots File
# Last Updated: May 2026
# Purpose: Allow search engines to crawl public pages; protect admin and checkout areas

User-agent: *
Allow: /
Allow: /blog/
Allow: /quiz/
Allow: /shop/
Allow: /pages/
Allow: /products/
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Disallow sensitive pages and directories
Disallow: /admin/
Disallow: /dashboard/
Disallow: /checkout/
Disallow: /cart/
Disallow: /account/
Disallow: /private/
Disallow: /api/
Disallow: /internal/
Disallow: /*.json$
Disallow: /*.pdf$
Disallow: /search?
Disallow: /*?*sort=
Disallow: /*?*filter=
Disallow: /temp/
Disallow: /backup/
Disallow: /cache/

# Allow specific bot behaviors
Allow: /robots.txt
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Crawl-Delay & Rate Limiting
Crawl-delay: 1
Request-rate: 10/1s

# Google-specific directives
User-agent: Googlebot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 0.5

# Bing-specific directives
User-agent: Bingbot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 1

# Disallow other bots (optional, strict mode)
User-agent: MJ12bot
User-agent: AhrefsBot
User-agent: SemrushBot
Disallow: /

# Sitemap location (critical for indexing)
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml
```

---

### 2.2 XML Sitemap Architecture

**Primary Sitemap (Main Index):**

**File:** `sitemap.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<sitemapindex xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">
  <!-- Main pages sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-main.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Blog/content sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Products/services sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Quiz landing pages sitemap (if quiz results create unique pages) -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-quiz.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
</sitemapindex>
```

**Main Pages Sitemap:**

**File:** `sitemap-main.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9"
        xmlns:image="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-image/1.1"
        xmlns:video="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-video/1.1
```


## License: unknown
https://github.com/juvenn/juvenn.github.io/blob/bc45aa1519558231d352b845e2301b5ba13e5cf7/src/routes/sitemap.xml/%2Bserver.js

```
# Comprehensive Design & Technical SEO Blueprint for Women's Wellness Website

---

## SECTION 1: Professional Female-Centric UI/UX Design & Branding

### 1.1 Visual Palette & Typography

**Color Palette (Modern, Premium, Wellness-Focused):**

| Color Role | Hex Code | RGB | Usage | Psychology |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Primary Brand** | `#8BA888` | (139, 168, 136) | Buttons, CTA, accents | Calming, natural, growth |
| **Secondary Accent** | `#B99B6B` | (185, 155, 107) | Highlights, badges, warmth | Luxury, grounding, trust |
| **Rose Accent** | `#D9876D` | (217, 135, 109) | Energy, urgency, passion | Movement, vitality, femininity |
| **Soft Lavender** | `#E8D9F0` | (232, 217, 240) | Subtle backgrounds, hover | Peace, rest, premium feel |
| **Warm Neutral (Bone)** | `#F5F1ED` | (245, 241, 237) | Page backgrounds, clean space | Modern, minimal, sophisticated |
| **Text (Ink)** | `#3D443D` | (61, 68, 61) | Body text, readability | Professional, grounded |
| **Muted Gray** | `#9A8E7E` | (154, 142, 126) | Secondary text, captions | Approachable, softer |

**Typography (Google Fonts Integration):**

```html
<!-- Add to <head> -->
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600;700&family=Playfair+Display:wght@600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
```

| Font | Role | Weight | Usage |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Playfair Display** | Serif Headline | 600–700 | Main headlines, hero section, premium feel |
| **Inter** | Sans-serif Body | 400–700 | Body text, CTAs, UI elements, readable at any size |

**Font Sizing Scale (Responsive):**
- **H1 (Hero):** 48px (mobile) → 64px (desktop)
- **H2 (Section):** 28px (mobile) → 42px (desktop)
- **H3 (Card Title):** 20px (mobile) → 24px (desktop)
- **Body:** 16px (mobile) → 18px (desktop)
- **Small Text:** 14px (mobile) → 16px (desktop)

---

### 1.2 Layout & Elements

**Landing Page Structure (High-Trust, Conversion-Optimized):**

```
1. HERO SECTION (Above the fold)
   ├─ Headline (Playfair Display, 64px, left-aligned)
   ├─ Subheading (Emotional, empathetic hook)
   ├─ Primary CTA Button (Sage green, 16px, rounded-full)
   ├─ Social Proof (Avatar stack + "50,000+ women reclaimed energy")
   └─ Hero Image (Right side, authentic woman, natural lighting, peaceful expression)

2. TRUST BADGES SECTION
   ├─ 5-star rating + review count (3,842 reviews)
   ├─ Verified checkmarks
   ├─ 30-day money-back guarantee badge
   └─ SSL/Security badge

3. PROBLEM-AGITATION SECTION
   ├─ "The Struggles Are Real" (H2)
   ├─ 3 pain-point cards with icons (Energy, Sleep, Confidence)
   └─ Emotional copy validating her struggles

4. SOLUTION-BENEFITS SECTION
   ├─ "Your Personalized Blueprint" (H2)
   ├─ 4 benefit cards (Energy, Sleep, Confidence, Body)
   └─ Light background color (Lavender or Bone)

5. HOW IT WORKS
   ├─ 3-step timeline (Quiz → Analysis → Personalized Plan)
   └─ Simple, clean icons + minimal copy

6. TESTIMONIALS / SOCIAL PROOF
   ├─ Before/After Slider (drag-to-compare)
   ├─ 3–6 testimonial cards (avatar, name, location, result, 5-star rating)
   └─ Video testimonial embed (optional, high-impact)

7. FAQ SECTION
   ├─ 5–7 collapsible accordion items
   └─ Common objection handlers (No diet, not restrictive, etc.)

8. FINAL CTA
   ├─ Bold headline ("Ready to Feel Like Yourself Again?")
   ├─ Primary button (Sage green, large, high contrast)
   └─ Guarantee statement (30-day money-back, no questions)
```

**Quiz Page Layout (Engagement-First):**

```
1. PROGRESS BAR
   ├─ Visual indicator (current question / total 13)
   └─ Percentage filled (0%–100%)

2. QUESTION CARD
   ├─ Large, readable question (20px–24px, Playfair or Inter)
   ├─ Supportive subtext (optional, smaller font)
   └─ Answer options (buttons, radio, slider—contextual)

3. ANSWER BUTTONS
   ├─ Light gray background (hover: sage green)
   ├─ Rounded corners (12px–16px border radius)
   ├─ Smooth transitions (250ms)
   └─ Mobile: full-width, stacked vertically

4. NAVIGATION
   ├─ "Back" button (quiet gray, left-aligned)
   ├─ "Next" / "Continue" button (sage green, prominent, right-aligned)
   └─ Mobile: bottom sticky bar with both buttons

5. EMOTIONAL PROGRESS
   ├─ Supportive microcopy ("You're doing great!")
   ├─ Progress celebrations (phases completed)
   └─ Optional progress emojis (✓, 🌱, 💪)
```

**Product / Service Cards (High-Converting):**

```
CARD STRUCTURE
├─ Image or icon (aspect ratio 3:2 or 16:9)
├─ Category badge (soft green background, small text)
├─ Title (H3, Playfair Display)
├─ Description (2–3 lines, 16px Inter)
├─ Primary benefit (italic, 14px, sage green text)
├─ Key features (3–5 bullet points, checkmark icons)
├─ Price section
│  ├─ Current price (large, bold, sage green)
│  ├─ Strikethrough old price (muted gray)
│  └─ Savings callout (rose red background)
├─ Trust badges (30-day guarantee, instant access, SSL)
└─ CTA button (Sage green, full-width on mobile)
```

  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Products/services sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Quiz landing pages sitemap (if quiz results create unique pages) -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-quiz.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
</sitemapindex>
```

**Main Pages Sitemap:**

**File:** `sitemap-main.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9"
        xmlns:image="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-image/1.1"
        xmlns:video="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-video/1.1">
  
  <!-- Homepage (highest
```

https://github.com/frogsystem/fs2core/blob/b2c7d2272127ef458dd81969b8be771af5beeb75/www/libs/feeds/sitemap.php

# Comprehensive Design & Technical SEO Blueprint for Women's Wellness Website

---

## SECTION 1: Professional Female-Centric UI/UX Design & Branding

### 1.1 Visual Palette & Typography

**Color Palette (Modern, Premium, Wellness-Focused):**

| Color Role | Hex Code | RGB | Usage | Psychology |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Primary Brand** | `#8BA888` | (139, 168, 136) | Buttons, CTA, accents | Calming, natural, growth |
| **Secondary Accent** | `#B99B6B` | (185, 155, 107) | Highlights, badges, warmth | Luxury, grounding, trust |
| **Rose Accent** | `#D9876D` | (217, 135, 109) | Energy, urgency, passion | Movement, vitality, femininity |
| **Soft Lavender** | `#E8D9F0` | (232, 217, 240) | Subtle backgrounds, hover | Peace, rest, premium feel |
| **Warm Neutral (Bone)** | `#F5F1ED` | (245, 241, 237) | Page backgrounds, clean space | Modern, minimal, sophisticated |
| **Text (Ink)** | `#3D443D` | (61, 68, 61) | Body text, readability | Professional, grounded |
| **Muted Gray** | `#9A8E7E` | (154, 142, 126) | Secondary text, captions | Approachable, softer |

**Typography (Google Fonts Integration):**

```html
<!-- Add to <head> -->
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600;700&family=Playfair+Display:wght@600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
```

| Font | Role | Weight | Usage |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Playfair Display** | Serif Headline | 600–700 | Main headlines, hero section, premium feel |
| **Inter** | Sans-serif Body | 400–700 | Body text, CTAs, UI elements, readable at any size |

**Font Sizing Scale (Responsive):**
- **H1 (Hero):** 48px (mobile) → 64px (desktop)
- **H2 (Section):** 28px (mobile) → 42px (desktop)
- **H3 (Card Title):** 20px (mobile) → 24px (desktop)
- **Body:** 16px (mobile) → 18px (desktop)
- **Small Text:** 14px (mobile) → 16px (desktop)

---

### 1.2 Layout & Elements

**Landing Page Structure (High-Trust, Conversion-Optimized):**

```
1. HERO SECTION (Above the fold)
   ├─ Headline (Playfair Display, 64px, left-aligned)
   ├─ Subheading (Emotional, empathetic hook)
   ├─ Primary CTA Button (Sage green, 16px, rounded-full)
   ├─ Social Proof (Avatar stack + "50,000+ women reclaimed energy")
   └─ Hero Image (Right side, authentic woman, natural lighting, peaceful expression)

2. TRUST BADGES SECTION
   ├─ 5-star rating + review count (3,842 reviews)
   ├─ Verified checkmarks
   ├─ 30-day money-back guarantee badge
   └─ SSL/Security badge

3. PROBLEM-AGITATION SECTION
   ├─ "The Struggles Are Real" (H2)
   ├─ 3 pain-point cards with icons (Energy, Sleep, Confidence)
   └─ Emotional copy validating her struggles

4. SOLUTION-BENEFITS SECTION
   ├─ "Your Personalized Blueprint" (H2)
   ├─ 4 benefit cards (Energy, Sleep, Confidence, Body)
   └─ Light background color (Lavender or Bone)

5. HOW IT WORKS
   ├─ 3-step timeline (Quiz → Analysis → Personalized Plan)
   └─ Simple, clean icons + minimal copy

6. TESTIMONIALS / SOCIAL PROOF
   ├─ Before/After Slider (drag-to-compare)
   ├─ 3–6 testimonial cards (avatar, name, location, result, 5-star rating)
   └─ Video testimonial embed (optional, high-impact)

7. FAQ SECTION
   ├─ 5–7 collapsible accordion items
   └─ Common objection handlers (No diet, not restrictive, etc.)

8. FINAL CTA
   ├─ Bold headline ("Ready to Feel Like Yourself Again?")
   ├─ Primary button (Sage green, large, high contrast)
   └─ Guarantee statement (30-day money-back, no questions)
```

**Quiz Page Layout (Engagement-First):**

```
1. PROGRESS BAR
   ├─ Visual indicator (current question / total 13)
   └─ Percentage filled (0%–100%)

2. QUESTION CARD
   ├─ Large, readable question (20px–24px, Playfair or Inter)
   ├─ Supportive subtext (optional, smaller font)
   └─ Answer options (buttons, radio, slider—contextual)

3. ANSWER BUTTONS
   ├─ Light gray background (hover: sage green)
   ├─ Rounded corners (12px–16px border radius)
   ├─ Smooth transitions (250ms)
   └─ Mobile: full-width, stacked vertically

4. NAVIGATION
   ├─ "Back" button (quiet gray, left-aligned)
   ├─ "Next" / "Continue" button (sage green, prominent, right-aligned)
   └─ Mobile: bottom sticky bar with both buttons

5. EMOTIONAL PROGRESS
   ├─ Supportive microcopy ("You're doing great!")
   ├─ Progress celebrations (phases completed)
   └─ Optional progress emojis (✓, 🌱, 💪)
```

**Product / Service Cards (High-Converting):**

```
CARD STRUCTURE
├─ Image or icon (aspect ratio 3:2 or 16:9)
├─ Category badge (soft green background, small text)
├─ Title (H3, Playfair Display)
├─ Description (2–3 lines, 16px Inter)
├─ Primary benefit (italic, 14px, sage green text)
├─ Key features (3–5 bullet points, checkmark icons)
├─ Price section
│  ├─ Current price (large, bold, sage green)
│  ├─ Strikethrough old price (muted gray)
│  └─ Savings callout (rose red background)
├─ Trust badges (30-day guarantee, instant access, SSL)
└─ CTA button (Sage green, full-width on mobile)
```

---

### 1.3 Media Guidelines

**Photography & Imagery:**

| Category | Style | Tone | Examples |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Hero Images** | Authentic, natural lighting, minimalist background | Peaceful, confident, real | Woman in yoga pose, sunrise in home, candid smile |
| **Testimonial Avatars** | Diverse body types, ages 25–55, genuine expressions | Relatable, warm, trustworthy | Real photos, no excessive filtering |
| **Before/After** | Dignified, empowering (not shocking), same clothing/angle | Transformation, progress, hope | Posture improvement, visible confidence, not just weight |
| **Icon Usage** | Minimalist line-drawn icons, sage green or rose | Friendly, modern, non-clinical | Energy (lightning bolt), sleep (moon), confidence (heart) |
| **Video Content** | 15–60 seconds, testimonials & quick demos | Authentic, fast-paced, captions included | Woman doing yoga, short results montage, testimonial |

**Image Optimization:**
- Format: WebP (primary), JPEG fallback
- Sizes: Serve responsive images (480px, 768px, 1200px, 1920px)
- Alt text: Descriptive, keyword-rich, actionable
- Lazy loading: Enable for below-fold images

**Typography in Images:**
- Overlay text: Use Playfair Display in white or sage green
- Contrast ratio: Minimum 4.5:1 for accessibility

---

## SECTION 2: Technical SEO, Indexing & Crawling Files

### 2.1 robots.txt File

**Purpose:** Allow search engines to crawl public pages while protecting sensitive areas.

**File Location:** `robots.txt` in the root directory (e.g., `https://yoursite.com/robots.txt`)

```plaintext
# FitFeky Robots File
# Last Updated: May 2026
# Purpose: Allow search engines to crawl public pages; protect admin and checkout areas

User-agent: *
Allow: /
Allow: /blog/
Allow: /quiz/
Allow: /shop/
Allow: /pages/
Allow: /products/
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Disallow sensitive pages and directories
Disallow: /admin/
Disallow: /dashboard/
Disallow: /checkout/
Disallow: /cart/
Disallow: /account/
Disallow: /private/
Disallow: /api/
Disallow: /internal/
Disallow: /*.json$
Disallow: /*.pdf$
Disallow: /search?
Disallow: /*?*sort=
Disallow: /*?*filter=
Disallow: /temp/
Disallow: /backup/
Disallow: /cache/

# Allow specific bot behaviors
Allow: /robots.txt
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Crawl-Delay & Rate Limiting
Crawl-delay: 1
Request-rate: 10/1s

# Google-specific directives
User-agent: Googlebot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 0.5

# Bing-specific directives
User-agent: Bingbot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 1

# Disallow other bots (optional, strict mode)
User-agent: MJ12bot
User-agent: AhrefsBot
User-agent: SemrushBot
Disallow: /

# Sitemap location (critical for indexing)
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml
```

---

### 2.2 XML Sitemap Architecture

**Primary Sitemap (Main Index):**

**File:** `sitemap.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<sitemapindex xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">
  <!-- Main pages sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-main.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Blog/content sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Products/services sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Quiz landing pages sitemap (if quiz results create unique pages) -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-quiz.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
</sitemapindex>
```

**Main Pages Sitemap:**

**File:** `sitemap-main.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9"
        xmlns:image="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-image/1.1"
        xmlns:video="http://
```

   └─ Simple, clean icons + minimal copy

6. TESTIMONIALS / SOCIAL PROOF
   ├─ Before/After Slider (drag-to-compare)
   ├─ 3–6 testimonial cards (avatar, name, location, result, 5-star rating)
   └─ Video testimonial embed (optional, high-impact)

7. FAQ SECTION
   ├─ 5–7 collapsible accordion items
   └─ Common objection handlers (No diet, not restrictive, etc.)

8. FINAL CTA
   ├─ Bold headline ("Ready to Feel Like Yourself Again?")
   ├─ Primary button (Sage green, large, high contrast)
   └─ Guarantee statement (30-day money-back, no questions)
```

**Quiz Page Layout (Engagement-First):**

```
1. PROGRESS BAR
   ├─ Visual indicator (current question / total 13)
   └─ Percentage filled (0%–100%)

2. QUESTION CARD
   ├─ Large, readable question (20px–24px, Playfair or Inter)
   ├─ Supportive subtext (optional, smaller font)
   └─ Answer options (buttons, radio, slider—contextual)

3. ANSWER BUTTONS
   ├─ Light gray background (hover: sage green)
   ├─ Rounded corners (12px–16px border radius)
   ├─ Smooth transitions (250ms)
   └─ Mobile: full-width, stacked vertically

4. NAVIGATION
   ├─ "Back" button (quiet gray, left-aligned)
   ├─ "Next" / "Continue" button (sage green, prominent, right-aligned)
   └─ Mobile: bottom sticky bar with both buttons

5. EMOTIONAL PROGRESS
   ├─ Supportive microcopy ("You're doing great!")
   ├─ Progress celebrations (phases completed)
   └─ Optional progress emojis (✓, 🌱, 💪)
```

**Product / Service Cards (High-Converting):**

```
CARD STRUCTURE
├─ Image or icon (aspect ratio 3:2 or 16:9)
├─ Category badge (soft green background, small text)
├─ Title (H3, Playfair Display)
├─ Description (2–3 lines, 16px Inter)
├─ Primary benefit (italic, 14px, sage green text)
├─ Key features (3–5 bullet points, checkmark icons)
├─ Price section
│  ├─ Current price (large, bold, sage green)
│  ├─ Strikethrough old price (muted gray)
│  └─ Savings callout (rose red background)
├─ Trust badges (30-day guarantee, instant access, SSL)
└─ CTA button (Sage green, full-width on mobile)
```

---

### 1.3 Media Guidelines

**Photography & Imagery:**

| Category | Style | Tone | Examples |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Hero Images** | Authentic, natural lighting, minimalist background | Peaceful, confident, real | Woman in yoga pose, sunrise in home, candid smile |
| **Testimonial Avatars** | Diverse body types, ages 25–55, genuine expressions | Relatable, warm, trustworthy | Real photos, no excessive filtering |
| **Before/After** | Dignified, empowering (not shocking), same clothing/angle | Transformation, progress, hope | Posture improvement, visible confidence, not just weight |
| **Icon Usage** | Minimalist line-drawn icons, sage green or rose | Friendly, modern, non-clinical | Energy (lightning bolt), sleep (moon), confidence (heart) |
| **Video Content** | 15–60 seconds, testimonials & quick demos | Authentic, fast-paced, captions included | Woman doing yoga, short results montage, testimonial |

**Image Optimization:**
- Format: WebP (primary), JPEG fallback
- Sizes: Serve responsive images (480px, 768px, 1200px, 1920px)
- Alt text: Descriptive, keyword-rich, actionable
- Lazy loading: Enable for below-fold images

**Typography in Images:**
- Overlay text: Use Playfair Display in white or sage green
- Contrast ratio: Minimum 4.5:1 for accessibility

---

## SECTION 2: Technical SEO, Indexing & Crawling Files

### 2.1 robots.txt File

**Purpose:** Allow search engines to crawl public pages while protecting sensitive areas.

**File Location:** `robots.txt` in the root directory (e.g., `https://yoursite.com/robots.txt`)

```plaintext
# FitFeky Robots File
# Last Updated: May 2026
# Purpose: Allow search engines to crawl public pages; protect admin and checkout areas

User-agent: *
Allow: /
Allow: /blog/
Allow: /quiz/
Allow: /shop/
Allow: /pages/
Allow: /products/
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Disallow sensitive pages and directories
Disallow: /admin/
Disallow: /dashboard/
Disallow: /checkout/
Disallow: /cart/
Disallow: /account/
Disallow: /private/
Disallow: /api/
Disallow: /internal/
Disallow: /*.json$
Disallow: /*.pdf$
Disallow: /search?
Disallow: /*?*sort=
Disallow: /*?*filter=
Disallow: /temp/
Disallow: /backup/
Disallow: /cache/

# Allow specific bot behaviors
Allow: /robots.txt
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Crawl-Delay & Rate Limiting
Crawl-delay: 1
Request-rate: 10/1s

# Google-specific directives
User-agent: Googlebot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 0.5

# Bing-specific directives
User-agent: Bingbot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 1

# Disallow other bots (optional, strict mode)
User-agent: MJ12bot
User-agent: AhrefsBot
User-agent: SemrushBot
Disallow: /

# Sitemap location (critical for indexing)
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml
```

---

### 2.2 XML Sitemap Architecture

**Primary Sitemap (Main Index):**

**File:** `sitemap.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<sitemapindex xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">
  <!-- Main pages sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-main.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Blog/content sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Products/services sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Quiz landing pages sitemap (if quiz results create unique pages) -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-quiz.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
</sitemapindex>
```

**Main Pages Sitemap:**

**File:** `sitemap-main.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9"
        xmlns:image="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-image/1.1"
        xmlns:video="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-video/1.1
```


## License: unknown
https://github.com/juvenn/juvenn.github.io/blob/bc45aa1519558231d352b845e2301b5ba13e5cf7/src/routes/sitemap.xml/%2Bserver.js

```
# Comprehensive Design & Technical SEO Blueprint for Women's Wellness Website

---

## SECTION 1: Professional Female-Centric UI/UX Design & Branding

### 1.1 Visual Palette & Typography

**Color Palette (Modern, Premium, Wellness-Focused):**

| Color Role | Hex Code | RGB | Usage | Psychology |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Primary Brand** | `#8BA888` | (139, 168, 136) | Buttons, CTA, accents | Calming, natural, growth |
| **Secondary Accent** | `#B99B6B` | (185, 155, 107) | Highlights, badges, warmth | Luxury, grounding, trust |
| **Rose Accent** | `#D9876D` | (217, 135, 109) | Energy, urgency, passion | Movement, vitality, femininity |
| **Soft Lavender** | `#E8D9F0` | (232, 217, 240) | Subtle backgrounds, hover | Peace, rest, premium feel |
| **Warm Neutral (Bone)** | `#F5F1ED` | (245, 241, 237) | Page backgrounds, clean space | Modern, minimal, sophisticated |
| **Text (Ink)** | `#3D443D` | (61, 68, 61) | Body text, readability | Professional, grounded |
| **Muted Gray** | `#9A8E7E` | (154, 142, 126) | Secondary text, captions | Approachable, softer |

**Typography (Google Fonts Integration):**

```html
<!-- Add to <head> -->
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600;700&family=Playfair+Display:wght@600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
```

| Font | Role | Weight | Usage |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Playfair Display** | Serif Headline | 600–700 | Main headlines, hero section, premium feel |
| **Inter** | Sans-serif Body | 400–700 | Body text, CTAs, UI elements, readable at any size |

**Font Sizing Scale (Responsive):**
- **H1 (Hero):** 48px (mobile) → 64px (desktop)
- **H2 (Section):** 28px (mobile) → 42px (desktop)
- **H3 (Card Title):** 20px (mobile) → 24px (desktop)
- **Body:** 16px (mobile) → 18px (desktop)
- **Small Text:** 14px (mobile) → 16px (desktop)

---

### 1.2 Layout & Elements

**Landing Page Structure (High-Trust, Conversion-Optimized):**

```
1. HERO SECTION (Above the fold)
   ├─ Headline (Playfair Display, 64px, left-aligned)
   ├─ Subheading (Emotional, empathetic hook)
   ├─ Primary CTA Button (Sage green, 16px, rounded-full)
   ├─ Social Proof (Avatar stack + "50,000+ women reclaimed energy")
   └─ Hero Image (Right side, authentic woman, natural lighting, peaceful expression)

2. TRUST BADGES SECTION
   ├─ 5-star rating + review count (3,842 reviews)
   ├─ Verified checkmarks
   ├─ 30-day money-back guarantee badge
   └─ SSL/Security badge

3. PROBLEM-AGITATION SECTION
   ├─ "The Struggles Are Real" (H2)
   ├─ 3 pain-point cards with icons (Energy, Sleep, Confidence)
   └─ Emotional copy validating her struggles

4. SOLUTION-BENEFITS SECTION
   ├─ "Your Personalized Blueprint" (H2)
   ├─ 4 benefit cards (Energy, Sleep, Confidence, Body)
   └─ Light background color (Lavender or Bone)

5. HOW IT WORKS
   ├─ 3-step timeline (Quiz → Analysis → Personalized Plan)
   └─ Simple, clean icons + minimal copy

6. TESTIMONIALS / SOCIAL PROOF
   ├─ Before/After Slider (drag-to-compare)
   ├─ 3–6 testimonial cards (avatar, name, location, result, 5-star rating)
   └─ Video testimonial embed (optional, high-impact)

7. FAQ SECTION
   ├─ 5–7 collapsible accordion items
   └─ Common objection handlers (No diet, not restrictive, etc.)

8. FINAL CTA
   ├─ Bold headline ("Ready to Feel Like Yourself Again?")
   ├─ Primary button (Sage green, large, high contrast)
   └─ Guarantee statement (30-day money-back, no questions)
```

   ├─ Visual indicator (current question / total 13)

   ├─ Smooth transitions (250ms)
   └─ Mobile: full-width, stacked vertically

   ├─ "Back" button (quiet gray, left-aligned)
   ├─ "Next" / "Continue" button (sage green, prominent, right-aligned)
   └─ Mobile: bottom sticky bar with both buttons

   ├─ Supportive microcopy ("You're doing great!")
   ├─ Progress celebrations (phases completed)
   └─ Optional progress emojis (✓, 🌱, 💪)
```

User-agent: Googlebot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 0.5

# Bing-specific directives
User-agent: Bingbot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 1

# Disallow other bots (optional, strict mode)
User-agent: MJ12bot
User-agent: AhrefsBot
User-agent: SemrushBot
Disallow: /

# Sitemap location (critical for indexing)
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml
```

---

### 2.2 XML Sitemap Architecture

**Primary Sitemap (Main Index):**

**File:** `sitemap.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<sitemapindex xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">
  <!-- Main pages sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-main.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Blog/content sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Products/services sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Quiz landing pages sitemap (if quiz results create unique pages) -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-quiz.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
</sitemapindex>
```

**Main Pages Sitemap:**

**File:** `sitemap-main.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9"
        xmlns:image="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-image/1.1"
        xmlns:video="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-video/1.1">
  
  <!-- Homepage (highest
```

https://github.com/frogsystem/fs2core/blob/b2c7d2272127ef458dd81969b8be771af5beeb75/www/libs/feeds/sitemap.php

```
# Comprehensive Design & Technical SEO Blueprint for Women's Wellness Website

---

## SECTION 1: Professional Female-Centric UI/UX Design & Branding

### 1.1 Visual Palette & Typography

**Color Palette (Modern, Premium, Wellness-Focused):**

| Color Role | Hex Code | RGB | Usage | Psychology |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Primary Brand** | `#8BA888` | (139, 168, 136) | Buttons, CTA, accents | Calming, natural, growth |
| **Secondary Accent** | `#B99B6B` | (185, 155, 107) | Highlights, badges, warmth | Luxury, grounding, trust |
| **Rose Accent** | `#D9876D` | (217, 135, 109) | Energy, urgency, passion | Movement, vitality, femininity |
| **Soft Lavender** | `#E8D9F0` | (232, 217, 240) | Subtle backgrounds, hover | Peace, rest, premium feel |
| **Warm Neutral (Bone)** | `#F5F1ED` | (245, 241, 237) | Page backgrounds, clean space | Modern, minimal, sophisticated |
| **Text (Ink)** | `#3D443D` | (61, 68, 61) | Body text, readability | Professional, grounded |
| **Muted Gray** | `#9A8E7E` | (154, 142, 126) | Secondary text, captions | Approachable, softer |

**Typography (Google Fonts Integration):**

```html
<!-- Add to <head> -->
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600;700&family=Playfair+Display:wght@600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
```

| Font | Role | Weight | Usage |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Playfair Display** | Serif Headline | 600–700 | Main headlines, hero section, premium feel |
| **Inter** | Sans-serif Body | 400–700 | Body text, CTAs, UI elements, readable at any size |

**Font Sizing Scale (Responsive):**
- **H1 (Hero):** 48px (mobile) → 64px (desktop)
- **H2 (Section):** 28px (mobile) → 42px (desktop)
- **H3 (Card Title):** 20px (mobile) → 24px (desktop)
- **Body:** 16px (mobile) → 18px (desktop)
- **Small Text:** 14px (mobile) → 16px (desktop)

---

### 1.2 Layout & Elements

**Landing Page Structure (High-Trust, Conversion-Optimized):**

```
1. HERO SECTION (Above the fold)
   ├─ Headline (Playfair Display, 64px, left-aligned)
   ├─ Subheading (Emotional, empathetic hook)
   ├─ Primary CTA Button (Sage green, 16px, rounded-full)
   ├─ Social Proof (Avatar stack + "50,000+ women reclaimed energy")
   └─ Hero Image (Right side, authentic woman, natural lighting, peaceful expression)

2. TRUST BADGES SECTION
   ├─ 5-star rating + review count (3,842 reviews)
   ├─ Verified checkmarks
   ├─ 30-day money-back guarantee badge
   └─ SSL/Security badge

3. PROBLEM-AGITATION SECTION
   ├─ "The Struggles Are Real" (H2)
   ├─ 3 pain-point cards with icons (Energy, Sleep, Confidence)
   └─ Emotional copy validating her struggles

4. SOLUTION-BENEFITS SECTION
   ├─ "Your Personalized Blueprint" (H2)
   ├─ 4 benefit cards (Energy, Sleep, Confidence, Body)
   └─ Light background color (Lavender or Bone)

5. HOW IT WORKS
   ├─ 3-step timeline (Quiz → Analysis → Personalized Plan)
   └─ Simple, clean icons + minimal copy

6. TESTIMONIALS / SOCIAL PROOF
   ├─ Before/After Slider (drag-to-compare)
   ├─ 3–6 testimonial cards (avatar, name, location, result, 5-star rating)
   └─ Video testimonial embed (optional, high-impact)

7. FAQ SECTION
   ├─ 5–7 collapsible accordion items
   └─ Common objection handlers (No diet, not restrictive, etc.)

8. FINAL CTA
   ├─ Bold headline ("Ready to Feel Like Yourself Again?")
   ├─ Primary button (Sage green, large, high contrast)
   └─ Guarantee statement (30-day money-back, no questions)
```

**Quiz Page Layout (Engagement-First):**

```
1. PROGRESS BAR
   ├─ Visual indicator (current question / total 13)
   └─ Percentage filled (0%–100%)

2. QUESTION CARD
   ├─ Large, readable question (20px–24px, Playfair or Inter)
   ├─ Supportive subtext (optional, smaller font)
   └─ Answer options (buttons, radio, slider—contextual)

3. ANSWER BUTTONS
   ├─ Light gray background (hover: sage green)
   ├─ Rounded corners (12px–16px border radius)
   ├─ Smooth transitions (250ms)
   └─ Mobile: full-width, stacked vertically

4. NAVIGATION
   ├─ "Back" button (quiet gray, left-aligned)
   ├─ "Next" / "Continue" button (sage green, prominent, right-aligned)
   └─ Mobile: bottom sticky bar with both buttons

5. EMOTIONAL PROGRESS
   ├─ Supportive microcopy ("You're doing great!")
   ├─ Progress celebrations (phases completed)
   └─ Optional progress emojis (✓, 🌱, 💪)
```

**Product / Service Cards (High-Converting):**

```
CARD STRUCTURE
├─ Image or icon (aspect ratio 3:2 or 16:9)
├─ Category badge (soft green background, small text)
├─ Title (H3, Playfair Display)
├─ Description (2–3 lines, 16px Inter)
├─ Primary benefit (italic, 14px, sage green text)
├─ Key features (3–5 bullet points, checkmark icons)
├─ Price section
│  ├─ Current price (large, bold, sage green)
│  ├─ Strikethrough old price (muted gray)
│  └─ Savings callout (rose red background)
├─ Trust badges (30-day guarantee, instant access, SSL)
└─ CTA button (Sage green, full-width on mobile)
```

---

### 1.3 Media Guidelines

**Photography & Imagery:**

| Category | Style | Tone | Examples |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Hero Images** | Authentic, natural lighting, minimalist background | Peaceful, confident, real | Woman in yoga pose, sunrise in home, candid smile |
| **Testimonial Avatars** | Diverse body types, ages 25–55, genuine expressions | Relatable, warm, trustworthy | Real photos, no excessive filtering |
| **Before/After** | Dignified, empowering (not shocking), same clothing/angle | Transformation, progress, hope | Posture improvement, visible confidence, not just weight |
| **Icon Usage** | Minimalist line-drawn icons, sage green or rose | Friendly, modern, non-clinical | Energy (lightning bolt), sleep (moon), confidence (heart) |
| **Video Content** | 15–60 seconds, testimonials & quick demos | Authentic, fast-paced, captions included | Woman doing yoga, short results montage, testimonial |

**Image Optimization:**
- Format: WebP (primary), JPEG fallback
- Sizes: Serve responsive images (480px, 768px, 1200px, 1920px)
- Alt text: Descriptive, keyword-rich, actionable
- Lazy loading: Enable for below-fold images

**Typography in Images:**
- Overlay text: Use Playfair Display in white or sage green
- Contrast ratio: Minimum 4.5:1 for accessibility

---

## SECTION 2: Technical SEO, Indexing & Crawling Files

### 2.1 robots.txt File

**Purpose:** Allow search engines to crawl public pages while protecting sensitive areas.

**File Location:** `robots.txt` in the root directory (e.g., `https://yoursite.com/robots.txt`)

```plaintext
# FitFeky Robots File
# Last Updated: May 2026
# Purpose: Allow search engines to crawl public pages; protect admin and checkout areas

User-agent: *
Allow: /
Allow: /blog/
Allow: /quiz/
Allow: /shop/
Allow: /pages/
Allow: /products/
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Disallow sensitive pages and directories
Disallow: /admin/
Disallow: /dashboard/
Disallow: /checkout/
Disallow: /cart/
Disallow: /account/
Disallow: /private/
Disallow: /api/
Disallow: /internal/
Disallow: /*.json$
Disallow: /*.pdf$
Disallow: /search?
Disallow: /*?*sort=
Disallow: /*?*filter=
Disallow: /temp/
Disallow: /backup/
Disallow: /cache/

# Allow specific bot behaviors
Allow: /robots.txt
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Crawl-Delay & Rate Limiting
Crawl-delay: 1
Request-rate: 10/1s

# Google-specific directives
User-agent: Googlebot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 0.5

# Bing-specific directives
User-agent: Bingbot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 1

# Disallow other bots (optional, strict mode)
User-agent: MJ12bot
User-agent: AhrefsBot
User-agent: SemrushBot
Disallow: /

# Sitemap location (critical for indexing)
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml
```

---

### 2.2 XML Sitemap Architecture

**Primary Sitemap (Main Index):**

**File:** `sitemap.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<sitemapindex xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">
  <!-- Main pages sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-main.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Blog/content sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Products/services sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Quiz landing pages sitemap (if quiz results create unique pages) -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-quiz.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
</sitemapindex>
```

**Main Pages Sitemap:**

**File:** `sitemap-main.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9"
        xmlns:image="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-image/1.1"
        xmlns:video="http://
```

```
1. HERO SECTION (Above the fold)
   ├─ Headline (Playfair Display, 64px, left-aligned)
   ├─ Subheading (Emotional, empathetic hook)
   ├─ Primary CTA Button (Sage green, 16px, rounded-full)
   ├─ Social Proof (Avatar stack + "50,000+ women reclaimed energy")
   └─ Hero Image (Right side, authentic woman, natural lighting, peaceful expression)

2. TRUST BADGES SECTION
   ├─ 5-star rating + review count (3,842 reviews)
   ├─ Verified checkmarks
   ├─ 30-day money-back guarantee badge
   └─ SSL/Security badge

3. PROBLEM-AGITATION SECTION
   ├─ "The Struggles Are Real" (H2)
   ├─ 3 pain-point cards with icons (Energy, Sleep, Confidence)
   └─ Emotional copy validating her struggles

4. SOLUTION-BENEFITS SECTION
   ├─ "Your Personalized Blueprint" (H2)
   ├─ 4 benefit cards (Energy, Sleep, Confidence, Body)
   └─ Light background color (Lavender or Bone)

5. HOW IT WORKS
   ├─ 3-step timeline (Quiz → Analysis → Personalized Plan)
   └─ Simple, clean icons + minimal copy

6. TESTIMONIALS / SOCIAL PROOF
   ├─ Before/After Slider (drag-to-compare)
   ├─ 3–6 testimonial cards (avatar, name, location, result, 5-star rating)
   └─ Video testimonial embed (optional, high-impact)

7. FAQ SECTION
   ├─ 5–7 collapsible accordion items
   └─ Common objection handlers (No diet, not restrictive, etc.)

8. FINAL CTA
   ├─ Bold headline ("Ready to Feel Like Yourself Again?")
   ├─ Primary button (Sage green, large, high contrast)
   └─ Guarantee statement (30-day money-back, no questions)
```

**Quiz Page Layout (Engagement-First):**

```
1. PROGRESS BAR
   ├─ Visual indicator (current question / total 13)
   └─ Percentage filled (0%–100%)

2. QUESTION CARD
   ├─ Large, readable question (20px–24px, Playfair or Inter)
   ├─ Supportive subtext (optional, smaller font)
   └─ Answer options (buttons, radio, slider—contextual)

3. ANSWER BUTTONS
   ├─ Light gray background (hover: sage green)
   ├─ Rounded corners (12px–16px border radius)
   ├─ Smooth transitions (250ms)
   └─ Mobile: full-width, stacked vertically

4. NAVIGATION
   ├─ "Back" button (quiet gray, left-aligned)
   ├─ "Next" / "Continue" button (sage green, prominent, right-aligned)
   └─ Mobile: bottom sticky bar with both buttons

5. EMOTIONAL PROGRESS
   ├─ Supportive microcopy ("You're doing great!")
   ├─ Progress celebrations (phases completed)
   └─ Optional progress emojis (✓, 🌱, 💪)
```

**Product / Service Cards (High-Converting):**

```
CARD STRUCTURE
├─ Image or icon (aspect ratio 3:2 or 16:9)
├─ Category badge (soft green background, small text)
├─ Title (H3, Playfair Display)
├─ Description (2–3 lines, 16px Inter)
├─ Primary benefit (italic, 14px, sage green text)
├─ Key features (3–5 bullet points, checkmark icons)
├─ Price section
│  ├─ Current price (large, bold, sage green)
│  ├─ Strikethrough old price (muted gray)
│  └─ Savings callout (rose red background)
├─ Trust badges (30-day guarantee, instant access, SSL)
└─ CTA button (Sage green, full-width on mobile)
```

---

### 1.3 Media Guidelines

**Photography & Imagery:**

| Category | Style | Tone | Examples |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Hero Images** | Authentic, natural lighting, minimalist background | Peaceful, confident, real | Woman in yoga pose, sunrise in home, candid smile |
| **Testimonial Avatars** | Diverse body types, ages 25–55, genuine expressions | Relatable, warm, trustworthy | Real photos, no excessive filtering |
| **Before/After** | Dignified, empowering (not shocking), same clothing/angle | Transformation, progress, hope | Posture improvement, visible confidence, not just weight |
| **Icon Usage** | Minimalist line-drawn icons, sage green or rose | Friendly, modern, non-clinical | Energy (lightning bolt), sleep (moon), confidence (heart) |
| **Video Content** | 15–60 seconds, testimonials & quick demos | Authentic, fast-paced, captions included | Woman doing yoga, short results montage, testimonial |

**Image Optimization:**
- Format: WebP (primary), JPEG fallback
- Sizes: Serve responsive images (480px, 768px, 1200px, 1920px)
- Alt text: Descriptive, keyword-rich, actionable
- Lazy loading: Enable for below-fold images

**Typography in Images:**
- Overlay text: Use Playfair Display in white or sage green
- Contrast ratio: Minimum 4.5:1 for accessibility

---

## SECTION 2: Technical SEO, Indexing & Crawling Files

### 2.1 robots.txt File

**Purpose:** Allow search engines to crawl public pages while protecting sensitive areas.

**File Location:** `robots.txt` in the root directory (e.g., `https://yoursite.com/robots.txt`)

```plaintext
# FitFeky Robots File
# Last Updated: May 2026
# Purpose: Allow search engines to crawl public pages; protect admin and checkout areas

User-agent: *
Allow: /
Allow: /blog/
Allow: /quiz/
Allow: /shop/
Allow: /pages/
Allow: /products/
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Disallow sensitive pages and directories
Disallow: /admin/
Disallow: /dashboard/
Disallow: /checkout/
Disallow: /cart/
Disallow: /account/
Disallow: /private/
Disallow: /api/
Disallow: /internal/
Disallow: /*.json$
Disallow: /*.pdf$
Disallow: /search?
Disallow: /*?*sort=
Disallow: /*?*filter=
Disallow: /temp/
Disallow: /backup/
Disallow: /cache/

# Allow specific bot behaviors
Allow: /robots.txt
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Crawl-Delay & Rate Limiting
Crawl-delay: 1
Request-rate: 10/1s

# Google-specific directives
User-agent: Googlebot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 0.5

# Bing-specific directives
User-agent: Bingbot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 1

# Disallow other bots (optional, strict mode)
User-agent: MJ12bot
User-agent: AhrefsBot
User-agent: SemrushBot
Disallow: /

# Sitemap location (critical for indexing)
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml
```

---

### 2.2 XML Sitemap Architecture

**Primary Sitemap (Main Index):**

**File:** `sitemap.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<sitemapindex xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">
  <!-- Main pages sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-main.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Blog/content sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Products/services sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Quiz landing pages sitemap (if quiz results create unique pages) -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-quiz.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
</sitemapindex>
```

**Main Pages Sitemap:**

**File:** `sitemap-main.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9"
        xmlns:image="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-image/1.1"
        xmlns:video="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-video/1.1
```


## License: unknown
https://github.com/juvenn/juvenn.github.io/blob/bc45aa1519558231d352b845e2301b5ba13e5cf7/src/routes/sitemap.xml/%2Bserver.js

```
# Comprehensive Design & Technical SEO Blueprint for Women's Wellness Website

---

## SECTION 1: Professional Female-Centric UI/UX Design & Branding

### 1.1 Visual Palette & Typography

**Color Palette (Modern, Premium, Wellness-Focused):**

| Color Role | Hex Code | RGB | Usage | Psychology |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Primary Brand** | `#8BA888` | (139, 168, 136) | Buttons, CTA, accents | Calming, natural, growth |
| **Secondary Accent** | `#B99B6B` | (185, 155, 107) | Highlights, badges, warmth | Luxury, grounding, trust |
| **Rose Accent** | `#D9876D` | (217, 135, 109) | Energy, urgency, passion | Movement, vitality, femininity |
| **Soft Lavender** | `#E8D9F0` | (232, 217, 240) | Subtle backgrounds, hover | Peace, rest, premium feel |
| **Warm Neutral (Bone)** | `#F5F1ED` | (245, 241, 237) | Page backgrounds, clean space | Modern, minimal, sophisticated |
| **Text (Ink)** | `#3D443D` | (61, 68, 61) | Body text, readability | Professional, grounded |
| **Muted Gray** | `#9A8E7E` | (154, 142, 126) | Secondary text, captions | Approachable, softer |

**Typography (Google Fonts Integration):**

```html
<!-- Add to <head> -->
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600;700&family=Playfair+Display:wght@600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
```

| Font | Role | Weight | Usage |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Playfair Display** | Serif Headline | 600–700 | Main headlines, hero section, premium feel |
| **Inter** | Sans-serif Body | 400–700 | Body text, CTAs, UI elements, readable at any size |

**Font Sizing Scale (Responsive):**
- **H1 (Hero):** 48px (mobile) → 64px (desktop)
- **H2 (Section):** 28px (mobile) → 42px (desktop)
- **H3 (Card Title):** 20px (mobile) → 24px (desktop)
- **Body:** 16px (mobile) → 18px (desktop)
- **Small Text:** 14px (mobile) → 16px (desktop)

---

### 2.1 robots.txt File

**Purpose:** Allow search engines to crawl public pages while protecting sensitive areas.

**File Location:** `robots.txt` in the root directory (e.g., `https://yoursite.com/robots.txt`)

```plaintext
# FitFeky Robots File
# Last Updated: May 2026
# Purpose: Allow search engines to crawl public pages; protect admin and checkout areas

User-agent: *
Allow: /
Allow: /blog/
Allow: /quiz/
Allow: /shop/
Allow: /pages/
Allow: /products/
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Disallow sensitive pages and directories
Disallow: /admin/
Disallow: /dashboard/
Disallow: /checkout/
Disallow: /cart/
Disallow: /account/
Disallow: /private/
Disallow: /api/
Disallow: /internal/
Disallow: /*.json$
Disallow: /*.pdf$
Disallow: /search?
Disallow: /*?*sort=
Disallow: /*?*filter=
Disallow: /temp/
Disallow: /backup/
Disallow: /cache/

# Allow specific bot behaviors
Allow: /robots.txt
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Crawl-Delay & Rate Limiting
Crawl-delay: 1
Request-rate: 10/1s

# Google-specific directives
User-agent: Googlebot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 0.5

# Bing-specific directives
User-agent: Bingbot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 1

# Disallow other bots (optional, strict mode)
User-agent: MJ12bot
User-agent: AhrefsBot
User-agent: SemrushBot
Disallow: /

# Sitemap location (critical for indexing)
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml
```

---

### 2.2 XML Sitemap Architecture

**Primary Sitemap (Main Index):**

**File:** `sitemap.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<sitemapindex xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9">
  <!-- Main pages sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-main.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Blog/content sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Products/services sitemap -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Quiz landing pages sitemap (if quiz results create unique pages) -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-quiz.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
</sitemapindex>
```

**Main Pages Sitemap:**

**File:** `sitemap-main.xml`

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<urlset xmlns="http://www.sitemaps.org/schemas/sitemap/0.9"
        xmlns:image="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-image/1.1"
        xmlns:video="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-video/1.1">
  
  <!-- Homepage (highest
```

https://github.com/frogsystem/fs2core/blob/b2c7d2272127ef458dd81969b8be771af5beeb75/www/libs/feeds/sitemap.php

```
# Comprehensive Design & Technical SEO Blueprint for Women's Wellness Website

---

## SECTION 1: Professional Female-Centric UI/UX Design & Branding

### 1.1 Visual Palette & Typography

**Color Palette (Modern, Premium, Wellness-Focused):**

| Color Role | Hex Code | RGB | Usage | Psychology |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Primary Brand** | `#8BA888` | (139, 168, 136) | Buttons, CTA, accents | Calming, natural, growth |
| **Secondary Accent** | `#B99B6B` | (185, 155, 107) | Highlights, badges, warmth | Luxury, grounding, trust |
| **Rose Accent** | `#D9876D` | (217, 135, 109) | Energy, urgency, passion | Movement, vitality, femininity |
| **Soft Lavender** | `#E8D9F0` | (232, 217, 240) | Subtle backgrounds, hover | Peace, rest, premium feel |
| **Warm Neutral (Bone)** | `#F5F1ED` | (245, 241, 237) | Page backgrounds, clean space | Modern, minimal, sophisticated |
| **Text (Ink)** | `#3D443D` | (61, 68, 61) | Body text, readability | Professional, grounded |
| **Muted Gray** | `#9A8E7E` | (154, 142, 126) | Secondary text, captions | Approachable, softer |

**Typography (Google Fonts Integration):**

```html
<!-- Add to <head> -->
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
<link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
<link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600;700&family=Playfair+Display:wght@600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
```

| Font | Role | Weight | Usage |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Playfair Display** | Serif Headline | 600–700 | Main headlines, hero section, premium feel |
| **Inter** | Sans-serif Body | 400–700 | Body text, CTAs, UI elements, readable at any size |

**Font Sizing Scale (Responsive):**
- **H1 (Hero):** 48px (mobile) → 64px (desktop)
- **H2 (Section):** 28px (mobile) → 42px (desktop)
- **H3 (Card Title):** 20px (mobile) → 24px (desktop)
- **Body:** 16px (mobile) → 18px (desktop)
- **Small Text:** 14px (mobile) → 16px (desktop)

---

### 1.2 Layout & Elements

**Landing Page Structure (High-Trust, Conversion-Optimized):**

```
1. HERO SECTION (Above the fold)
   ├─ Headline (Playfair Display, 64px, left-aligned)
   ├─ Subheading (Emotional, empathetic hook)
   ├─ Primary CTA Button (Sage green, 16px, rounded-full)
   ├─ Social Proof (Avatar stack + "50,000+ women reclaimed energy")
   └─ Hero Image (Right side, authentic woman, natural lighting, peaceful expression)

2. TRUST BADGES SECTION
   ├─ 5-star rating + review count (3,842 reviews)
   ├─ Verified checkmarks
   ├─ 30-day money-back guarantee badge
   └─ SSL/Security badge

3. PROBLEM-AGITATION SECTION
   ├─ "The Struggles Are Real" (H2)
   ├─ 3 pain-point cards with icons (Energy, Sleep, Confidence)
   └─ Emotional copy validating her struggles

4. SOLUTION-BENEFITS SECTION
   ├─ "Your Personalized Blueprint" (H2)
   ├─ 4 benefit cards (Energy, Sleep, Confidence, Body)
   └─ Light background color (Lavender or Bone)

5. HOW IT WORKS
   ├─ 3-step timeline (Quiz → Analysis → Personalized Plan)
   └─ Simple, clean icons + minimal copy

6. TESTIMONIALS / SOCIAL PROOF
   ├─ Before/After Slider (drag-to-compare)
   ├─ 3–6 testimonial cards (avatar, name, location, result, 5-star rating)
   └─ Video testimonial embed (optional, high-impact)

7. FAQ SECTION
   ├─ 5–7 collapsible accordion items
   └─ Common objection handlers (No diet, not restrictive, etc.)

8. FINAL CTA
   ├─ Bold headline ("Ready to Feel Like Yourself Again?")
   ├─ Primary button (Sage green, large, high contrast)
   └─ Guarantee statement (30-day money-back, no questions)
```

**Quiz Page Layout (Engagement-First):**

```
1. PROGRESS BAR
   ├─ Visual indicator (current question / total 13)
   └─ Percentage filled (0%–100%)

2. QUESTION CARD
   ├─ Large, readable question (20px–24px, Playfair or Inter)
   ├─ Supportive subtext (optional, smaller font)
   └─ Answer options (buttons, radio, slider—contextual)

3. ANSWER BUTTONS
   ├─ Light gray background (hover: sage green)
   ├─ Rounded corners (12px–16px border radius)
   ├─ Smooth transitions (250ms)
   └─ Mobile: full-width, stacked vertically

4. NAVIGATION
   ├─ "Back" button (quiet gray, left-aligned)
   ├─ "Next" / "Continue" button (sage green, prominent, right-aligned)
   └─ Mobile: bottom sticky bar with both buttons

5. EMOTIONAL PROGRESS
   ├─ Supportive microcopy ("You're doing great!")
   ├─ Progress celebrations (phases completed)
   └─ Optional progress emojis (✓, 🌱, 💪)
```

**Product / Service Cards (High-Converting):**

```
CARD STRUCTURE
├─ Image or icon (aspect ratio 3:2 or 16:9)
├─ Category badge (soft green background, small text)
├─ Title (H3, Playfair Display)
├─ Description (2–3 lines, 16px Inter)
├─ Primary benefit (italic, 14px, sage green text)
├─ Key features (3–5 bullet points, checkmark icons)
├─ Price section
│  ├─ Current price (large, bold, sage green)
│  ├─ Strikethrough old price (muted gray)
│  └─ Savings callout (rose red background)
├─ Trust badges (30-day guarantee, instant access, SSL)
└─ CTA button (Sage green, full-width on mobile)
```

---

### 1.3 Media Guidelines

**Photography & Imagery:**

| Category | Style | Tone | Examples |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Hero Images** | Authentic, natural lighting, minimalist background | Peaceful, confident, real | Woman in yoga pose, sunrise in home, candid smile |
| **Testimonial Avatars** | Diverse body types, ages 25–55, genuine expressions | Relatable, warm, trustworthy | Real photos, no excessive filtering |
| **Before/After** | Dignified, empowering (not shocking), same clothing/angle | Transformation, progress, hope | Posture improvement, visible confidence, not just weight |
| **Icon Usage** | Minimalist line-drawn icons, sage green or rose | Friendly, modern, non-clinical | Energy (lightning bolt), sleep (moon), confidence (heart) |
| **Video Content** | 15–60 seconds, testimonials & quick demos | Authentic, fast-paced, captions included | Woman doing yoga, short results montage, testimonial |

**Image Optimization:**
- Format: WebP (primary), JPEG fallback
- Sizes: Serve responsive images (480px, 768px, 1200px, 1920px)
- Alt text: Descriptive, keyword-rich, actionable
- Lazy loading: Enable for below-fold images

**Typography in Images:**
- Overlay text: Use Playfair Display in white or sage green
- Contrast ratio: Minimum 4.5:1 for accessibility

---

## SECTION 2: Technical SEO, Indexing & Crawling Files

### 2.1 robots.txt File

**Purpose:** Allow search engines to crawl public pages while protecting sensitive areas.

**File Location:** `robots.txt` in the root directory (e.g., `https://yoursite.com/robots.txt`)

```plaintext
# FitFeky Robots File
# Last Updated: May 2026
# Purpose: Allow search engines to crawl public pages; protect admin and checkout areas

User-agent: *
Allow: /
Allow: /blog/
Allow: /quiz/
Allow: /shop/
Allow: /pages/
Allow: /products/
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Disallow sensitive pages and directories
Disallow: /admin/
Disallow: /dashboard/
Disallow: /checkout/
Disallow: /cart/
Disallow: /account/
Disallow: /private/
Disallow: /api/
Disallow: /internal/
Disallow: /*.json$
Disallow: /*.pdf$
Disallow: /search?
Disallow: /*?*sort=
Disallow: /*?*filter=
Disallow: /temp/
Disallow: /backup/
Disallow: /cache/

# Allow specific bot behaviors
Allow: /robots.txt
Allow: /sitemap.xml

# Crawl-Delay & Rate Limiting
Crawl-delay: 1
Request-rate: 10/1s

# Google-specific directives
User-agent: Googlebot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 0.5

# Bing-specific directives
User-agent: Bingbot
Allow: /
Crawl-delay: 1

# Disallow other bots (optional, strict mode)
User-agent: MJ12bot
User-agent: AhrefsBot
User-agent: SemrushBot
Disallow: /

# Sitemap location (critical for indexing)
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml
Sitemap: https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml
```

    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-blog.xml</loc>

    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-products.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>
  </sitemap>
  
  <!-- Quiz landing pages sitemap (if quiz results create unique pages) -->
  <sitemap>
    <loc>https://yoursite.com/sitemap-quiz.xml</loc>
    <lastmod>2026-05-22T00:00:00+00:00</lastmod>

        xmlns:video="http://www.google.com/schemas/sitemap-video/1.1
```
